</div></div></div></div><div id="tag/orgs" data-section-id="tag/orgs" class="sc-eCApnc lpoiLM"><div class="sc-iCoGMd fStpoi"><div class="sc-hKFxyN bwFyQs"><h1 class="sc-fujyAs bpZWeL"><a class="sc-crzoAE iUxAWq" href="#tag/orgs" aria-label="tag/orgs"></a>/orgs</h1></div></div><div class="sc-hKFxyN lksXXu"><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr QGruV redoc-markdown "><p>Team sites and personal spaces are called &#39;orgs&#39; in the API.</p>

</span></button></div></div></div><div class="sc-jSFjdj sc-gKAaRy bummOK gcushC"></div></div></div><div id="tag/records" data-section-id="tag/records" class="sc-eCApnc lpoiLM"><div class="sc-iCoGMd fStpoi"><div class="sc-hKFxyN bwFyQs"><h1 class="sc-fujyAs bpZWeL"><a class="sc-crzoAE iUxAWq" href="#tag/records" aria-label="tag/records"></a>/records</h1></div></div><div class="sc-hKFxyN lksXXu"><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr QGruV redoc-markdown "><p>Tables contain collections of records (also called rows).</p>
</div></div></div><div id="tag/records/paths/~1docs~1{docId}~1tables~1{tableId}~1records/get" data-section-id="tag/records/paths/~1docs~1{docId}~1tables~1{tableId}~1records/get" class="sc-eCApnc khndJD"><div class="sc-iCoGMd fStpoi"><div class="sc-hKFxyN bwFyQs"><h2 class="sc-pNWdM eftmgB"><a class="sc-crzoAE iUxAWq" href="#tag/records/paths/~1docs~1{docId}~1tables~1{tableId}~1records/get" aria-label="tag/records/paths/~1docs~1{docId}~1tables~1{tableId}~1records/get"></a>Fetch records from a table<!-- --> </h2><div class="sc-EZqKI fWsqvQ"><button class="sc-eEVmNe hyDbyC"><span type="get" class="sc-fmdNqN ihNycv http-verb get">get</span><span class="sc-jXcxbT fCEUju">/docs/{docId}/tables/{tableId}/records</span><svg class="sc-dIsUp izTTdU" style="margin-right:-25px" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 24 24" x="0" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" y="0" aria-hidden="true"><polygon points="17.3 8.3 12 13.6 6.7 8.3 5.3 9.7 12 16.4 18.7 9.7 "></polygon></svg></button><div aria-hidden="true" class="sc-ljsmAU flIrdF"><div class="sc-jlZJtj fQkroN"><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr lhENGb"></div><div tabindex="0" role="button"><div class="sc-dTSzeu dfUAUz"><span>https://docs.getgrist.com/api</span>/docs/{docId}/tables/{tableId}/records</div></div></div><div class="sc-jlZJtj fQkroN"><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr lhENGb"></div><div tabindex="0" role="button"><div class="sc-dTSzeu dfUAUz"><span>https://&lt;TEAM&gt;.getgrist.com/api</span>/docs/{docId}/tables/{tableId}/records</div></div></div></div></div><div class="sc-fcmMJX cvfxAX"><div class="sc-jUfyBS bhDyou"><h5 class="sc-iqAclL sc-fuISkM eONCmm hZIgic">Authorizations:</h5><svg class="sc-dIsUp iPqByX" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 24 24" x="0" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" y="0" aria-hidden="true"><polygon points="17.3 8.3 12 13.6 6.7 8.3 5.3 9.7 12 16.4 18.7 9.7 "></polygon></svg></div><div class="sc-jQAxuV ccffaZ"><span class="sc-daBunf fcvuS"><span class="sc-dsXzNU dPrSxx"><i>API Key</i></span></span></div></div><div><h5 class="sc-iqAclL eONCmm">path<!-- --> Parameters</h5><table class="sc-hHEiqL VCQHZ"><tbody><tr class=""><td class="sc-hBMUJo sc-fFSPTT iwcKgn cAqMTE" kind="field" title="docId"><span class="sc-iemWCZ bcnRwz"></span><span class="property-name">docId</span><div class="sc-oeezt sc-hhIiOg dLCGMn hIkHYw">required</div></td><td class="sc-bkbkJK ctPuOP"><div><div><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-iNiQyp jWaWWE jrLlAa"></span><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-jffHpj jWaWWE cThoNa">string</span><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-eJocfa jWaWWE bArHDh"> (<!-- -->DocKey<!-- -->) </span></div> <div><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr lhENGb"><p>A string id (UUID)</p>
</div></div></div></td></tr><tr class="last "><td class="sc-hBMUJo sc-fFSPTT iwcKgn cAqMTE" kind="field" title="tableId"><span class="sc-iemWCZ bcnRwz"></span><span class="property-name">tableId</span><div class="sc-oeezt sc-hhIiOg dLCGMn hIkHYw">required</div></td><td class="sc-bkbkJK ctPuOP"><div><div><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-iNiQyp jWaWWE jrLlAa"></span><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-jffHpj jWaWWE cThoNa">string</span></div> <div><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr lhENGb"><p>name of a table (normalized)</p>
</div></div></div></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div><h5 class="sc-iqAclL eONCmm">query<!-- --> Parameters</h5><table class="sc-hHEiqL VCQHZ"><tbody><tr class=""><td class="sc-hBMUJo sc-fFSPTT iwcKgn cAqMTE" kind="field" title="filter"><span class="sc-iemWCZ bcnRwz"></span><span class="property-name">filter</span></td><td class="sc-bkbkJK ctPuOP"><div><div><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-iNiQyp jWaWWE jrLlAa"></span><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-jffHpj jWaWWE cThoNa">string</span></div> <div><span class="sc-laZMeE jWaWWE"> <!-- -->Example:<!-- --> </span> <span class="sc-laZMeE sc-ckTSus jWaWWE fElSEN">filter={&quot;pet&quot;: [&quot;cat&quot;, &quot;dog&quot;]}</span></div><div><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr lhENGb"><p>This is a JSON object mapping column names to arrays of allowed values.  For example, to filter column <code>pet</code> for values <code>cat</code> and <code>dog</code>, the filter would be <code>{&quot;pet&quot;: [&quot;cat&quot;, &quot;dog&quot;]}</code>. JSON contains characters that are not safe to place in a URL, so it is important to url-encode them.  For this example, the url-encoding is <code>%7B%22pet%22%3A%20%5B%22cat%22%2C%20%22dog%22%5D%7D</code>. See <a href="https://rosettacode.org/wiki/URL_encoding">https://rosettacode.org/wiki/URL_encoding</a> for how to url-encode a string, or <a href="https://www.urlencoder.org/">https://www.urlencoder.org/</a> to try some examples. Multiple columns can be filtered. For example the filter for <code>pet</code> being either <code>cat</code> or <code>dog</code>, AND <code>size</code> being either <code>tiny</code> or <code>outrageously small</code>, would be <code>{&quot;pet&quot;: [&quot;cat&quot;, &quot;dog&quot;], &quot;size&quot;: [&quot;tiny&quot;, &quot;outrageously small&quot;]}</code>.</p>
</div></div></div></td></tr><tr class=""><td class="sc-hBMUJo sc-fFSPTT iwcKgn cAqMTE" kind="field" title="sort"><span class="sc-iemWCZ bcnRwz"></span><span class="property-name">sort</span></td><td class="sc-bkbkJK ctPuOP"><div><div><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-iNiQyp jWaWWE jrLlAa"></span><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-jffHpj jWaWWE cThoNa">string</span></div> <div><span class="sc-laZMeE jWaWWE"> <!-- -->Example:<!-- --> </span> <span class="sc-laZMeE sc-ckTSus jWaWWE fElSEN">sort=pet,-age</span></div><div><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr lhENGb"><p>Order in which to return results. If a single column name is given (e.g. <code>pet</code>), results are placed in ascending order of values in that column. To get results in an order that was previously prepared manually in Grist, use the special <code>manualSort</code> column name. Multiple columns can be specified, separated by commas (e.g. <code>pet,age</code>). For descending order, prefix a column name with a <code>-</code> character (e.g. <code>pet,-age</code>). To include additional sorting options append them after a colon (e.g. <code>pet,-age:naturalSort;emptyFirst,owner</code>). Available options are: <code>choiceOrder</code>, <code>naturalSort</code>, <code>emptyFirst</code>. Without the <code>sort</code> parameter, the order of results is unspecified.</p>
</div></div></div></td></tr><tr class="last "><td class="sc-hBMUJo sc-fFSPTT iwcKgn cAqMTE" kind="field" title="limit"><span class="sc-iemWCZ bcnRwz"></span><span class="property-name">limit</span></td><td class="sc-bkbkJK ctPuOP"><div><div><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-iNiQyp jWaWWE jrLlAa"></span><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-jffHpj jWaWWE cThoNa">number</span></div> <div><span class="sc-laZMeE jWaWWE"> <!-- -->Example:<!-- --> </span> <span class="sc-laZMeE sc-ckTSus jWaWWE fElSEN">limit=5</span></div><div><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr lhENGb"><p>Return at most this number of rows.  A value of 0 is equivalent to having no limit.</p>
</div></div></div></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div><h5 class="sc-iqAclL eONCmm">header<!-- --> Parameters</h5><table class="sc-hHEiqL VCQHZ"><tbody><tr class=""><td class="sc-hBMUJo sc-fFSPTT iwcKgn cAqMTE" kind="field" title="X-Sort"><span class="sc-iemWCZ bcnRwz"></span><span class="property-name">X-Sort</span></td><td class="sc-bkbkJK ctPuOP"><div><div><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-iNiQyp jWaWWE jrLlAa"></span><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-jffHpj jWaWWE cThoNa">string</span></div> <div><span class="sc-laZMeE jWaWWE"> <!-- -->Example:<!-- --> </span> <span class="sc-laZMeE sc-ckTSus jWaWWE fElSEN">pet,-age</span></div><div><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr lhENGb"><p>Same as <code>sort</code> query parameter.</p>
</div></div></div></td></tr><tr class="last "><td class="sc-hBMUJo sc-fFSPTT iwcKgn cAqMTE" kind="field" title="X-Limit"><span class="sc-iemWCZ bcnRwz"></span><span class="property-name">X-Limit</span></td><td class="sc-bkbkJK ctPuOP"><div><div><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-iNiQyp jWaWWE jrLlAa"></span><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-jffHpj jWaWWE cThoNa">number</span></div> <div><span class="sc-laZMeE jWaWWE"> <!-- -->Example:<!-- --> </span> <span class="sc-laZMeE sc-ckTSus jWaWWE fElSEN">5</span></div><div><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr lhENGb"><p>Same as <code>limit</code> query parameter.</p>
</div></div></div></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div><h3 class="sc-fIxmyt DvFer">Responses</h3><div><button class="sc-htmcrh lbYftx"><svg class="sc-dIsUp dqYXmg" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 24 24" x="0" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" y="0" aria-hidden="true"><polygon points="17.3 8.3 12 13.6 6.7 8.3 5.3 9.7 12 16.4 18.7 9.7 "></polygon></svg><strong class="sc-fWWYYk cMoEZ">200<!-- --> </strong><span class="sc-jcwpoC eDjFAZ"><p>Records from the table</p>

</div></div></div></td></tr><tr class=""><td class="sc-hBMUJo sc-fFSPTT iwcKgn cAqMTE" kind="field" title="onmany"><span class="sc-iemWCZ bcnRwz"></span><span class="property-name">onmany</span></td><td class="sc-bkbkJK ctPuOP"><div><div><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-iNiQyp jWaWWE jrLlAa"></span><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-jffHpj jWaWWE cThoNa">string</span></div><div><span class="sc-laZMeE jWaWWE"> <!-- -->Enum<!-- -->:</span> <span class="sc-laZMeE sc-ckTSus jWaWWE fElSEN">&quot;first&quot;</span> <span class="sc-laZMeE sc-ckTSus jWaWWE fElSEN">&quot;none&quot;</span> <span class="sc-laZMeE sc-ckTSus jWaWWE fElSEN">&quot;all&quot;</span> </div> <div><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr lhENGb"><p>Which records to update if multiple records are found to match <code>require</code>.</p>
<ul>
<li><code>first</code> - the first matching record (default)</li>
<li><code>none</code> - do not update anything</li>
<li><code>all</code> - update all matches</li>
</ul>
</div></div></div></td></tr><tr class=""><td class="sc-hBMUJo sc-fFSPTT iwcKgn cAqMTE" kind="field" title="noadd"><span class="sc-iemWCZ bcnRwz"></span><span class="property-name">noadd</span></td><td class="sc-bkbkJK ctPuOP"><div><div><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-iNiQyp jWaWWE jrLlAa"></span><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-jffHpj jWaWWE cThoNa">boolean</span></div> <div><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr lhENGb"><p>Set to true to prohibit adding records.</p>
</div></div></div></td></tr><tr class=""><td class="sc-hBMUJo sc-fFSPTT iwcKgn cAqMTE" kind="field" title="noupdate"><span class="sc-iemWCZ bcnRwz"></span><span class="property-name">noupdate</span></td><td class="sc-bkbkJK ctPuOP"><div><div><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-iNiQyp jWaWWE jrLlAa"></span><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-jffHpj jWaWWE cThoNa">boolean</span></div> <div><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr lhENGb"><p>Set to true to prohibit updating records.</p>
</div></div></div></td></tr><tr class="last "><td class="sc-hBMUJo sc-fFSPTT iwcKgn cAqMTE" kind="field" title="allow_empty_require"><span class="sc-iemWCZ bcnRwz"></span><span class="property-name">allow_empty_require</span></td><td class="sc-bkbkJK ctPuOP"><div><div><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-iNiQyp jWaWWE jrLlAa"></span><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-jffHpj jWaWWE cThoNa">boolean</span></div> <div><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr lhENGb"><p>Set to true to allow <code>require</code> in the body to be empty, which will match and update all records in the table.</p>
</div></div></div></td></tr></tbody></table></div><h5 class="sc-iqAclL eONCmm">Request Body schema: <span class="sc-cBoqAE eKyrDP">application/json</span></h5><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr QGruV"><p>The records to add or update. Instead of an id, a <code>require</code> object is provided, with the same structure as <code>fields</code>. If no query parameter options are set, then the operation is as follows. First, we check if a record exists matching the values specified for columns in <code>require</code>. If so, we update it by setting the values specified for columns in <code>fields</code>. If not, we create a new record with a combination of the values in <code>require</code> and <code>fields</code>, with <code>fields</code> taking priority if the same column is specified in both. The query parameters allow for variations on this behavior.</p>
</div><table class="sc-hHEiqL VCQHZ"><tbody><tr class="last "><td class="sc-hBMUJo sc-fFSPTT sc-gSYDnn iwcKgn cAqMTE hTttpy" kind="field" title="records"><span class="sc-iemWCZ bcnRwz"></span><button aria-label="expand properties"><span class="property-name">records</span><svg class="sc-dIsUp hGHhhO" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 24 24" x="0" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" y="0" aria-hidden="true"><polygon points="17.3 8.3 12 13.6 6.7 8.3 5.3 9.7 12 16.4 18.7 9.7 "></polygon></svg></button><div class="sc-oeezt sc-hhIiOg dLCGMn hIkHYw">required</div></td><td class="sc-bkbkJK ctPuOP"><div><div><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-iNiQyp jWaWWE jrLlAa">Array of </span><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-jffHpj jWaWWE cThoNa">objects</span></div> <div><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr lhENGb"></div></div></div></td></tr></tbody></table><div><h3 class="sc-fIxmyt DvFer">Responses</h3><div><button class="sc-htmcrh jUGDyD" disabled=""><strong class="sc-fWWYYk cMoEZ">200<!-- --> </strong><span class="sc-jcwpoC eDjFAZ"><p>Success</p>
</span></button></div></div></div><div class="sc-jSFjdj sc-gKAaRy bummOK gcushC"><div><h3 class="sc-kEqXSa iXmHCl"> <!-- -->Request samples<!-- --> </h3><div class="sc-cxNHIi gxohHo" data-rttabs="true"><ul class="react-tabs__tab-list" role="tablist"><li class="react-tabs__tab react-tabs__tab--selected" role="tab" id="react-tabs-46" aria-selected="true" aria-disabled="false" aria-labelledby="react-tabs-48"><div><div class="sc-Arkif jojbRz"><span class="sc-cOifOu hlhNtL">Content type</span><div class="sc-bBjRSN kQSIAz">application/json</div></div><div class="sc-jgPyTC dSaTNC"><div class="sc-jNnpgg esZIbL"><div class="sc-giAqHp hMPeqJ"><button><div class="sc-carFqZ UksDl">Copy</div></button><button> Expand all </button><button> Collapse all </button></div><div class="sc-iJCRrE jCdxGr sc-dPaNzc gyljjx"><div class="redoc-json"><code><button class="collapser" aria-label="collapse"></button><span class="token punctuation">{</span><span class="sc-eCApnc lpoiLM"><div class="sc-iCoGMd fStpoi"><div class="sc-hKFxyN bwFyQs"><h1 class="sc-fujyAs bpZWeL"><a class="sc-crzoAE iUxAWq" href="#tag/data" aria-label="tag/data"></a>/data</h1></div></div><div class="sc-hKFxyN lksXXu"><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr QGruV redoc-markdown "><p>Work with table data, using a (now deprecated) columnar format. We now recommend the <code>records</code> endpoints.</p>
</div></div></div><div id="tag/data/paths/~1docs~1{docId}~1tables~1{tableId}~1data/get" data-section-id="tag/data/paths/~1docs~1{docId}~1tables~1{tableId}~1data/get" class="sc-eCApnc khndJD"><div class="sc-iCoGMd fStpoi"><div class="sc-hKFxyN bwFyQs"><h2 class="sc-pNWdM eftmgB"><a class="sc-crzoAE iUxAWq" href="#tag/data/paths/~1docs~1{docId}~1tables~1{tableId}~1data/get" aria-label="tag/data/paths/~1docs~1{docId}~1tables~1{tableId}~1data/get"></a>Fetch data from a table<!-- --> <span type="warning" class="sc-bqGGPW eSYQnm"> Deprecated </span></h2><div class="sc-EZqKI fWsqvQ"><button class="sc-eEVmNe hyDbyC"><span type="get" class="sc-fmdNqN ihNycv http-verb get">get</span><span class="sc-jXcxbT fCEUju">/docs/{docId}/tables/{tableId}/data</span><svg class="sc-dIsUp izTTdU" style="margin-right:-25px" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 24 24" x="0" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" y="0" aria-hidden="true"><polygon points="17.3 8.3 12 13.6 6.7 8.3 5.3 9.7 12 16.4 18.7 9.7 "></polygon></svg></button><div aria-hidden="true" class="sc-ljsmAU flIrdF"><div class="sc-jlZJtj fQkroN"><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr lhENGb"></div><div tabindex="0" role="button"><div class="sc-dTSzeu dfUAUz"><span>https://docs.getgrist.com/api</span>/docs/{docId}/tables/{tableId}/data</div></div></div><div class="sc-jlZJtj fQkroN"><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr lhENGb"></div><div tabindex="0" role="button"><div class="sc-dTSzeu dfUAUz"><span>https://&lt;TEAM&gt;.getgrist.com/api</span>/docs/{docId}/tables/{tableId}/data</div></div></div></div></div><div class="sc-iGkqmO hCTIhr"><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr QGruV"><p>Deprecated in favor of <code>records</code> endpoints. We have no immediate plans to remove these endpoints, but consider <code>records</code> a better starting point for new projects.</p>
</div></div><div class="sc-fcmMJX cvfxAX"><div class="sc-jUfyBS bhDyou"><h5 class="sc-iqAclL sc-fuISkM eONCmm hZIgic">Authorizations:</h5><svg class="sc-dIsUp iPqByX" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 24 24" x="0" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" y="0" aria-hidden="true"><polygon points="17.3 8.3 12 13.6 6.7 8.3 5.3 9.7 12 16.4 18.7 9.7 "></polygon></svg></div><div class="sc-jQAxuV ccffaZ"><span class="sc-daBunf fcvuS"><span class="sc-dsXzNU dPrSxx"><i>API Key</i></span></span></div></div><div><h5 class="sc-iqAclL eONCmm">path<!-- --> Parameters</h5><table class="sc-hHEiqL VCQHZ"><tbody><tr class=""><td class="sc-hBMUJo sc-fFSPTT iwcKgn cAqMTE" kind="field" title="docId"><span class="sc-iemWCZ bcnRwz"></span><span class="property-name">docId</span><div class="sc-oeezt sc-hhIiOg dLCGMn hIkHYw">required</div></td><td class="sc-bkbkJK ctPuOP"><div><div><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-iNiQyp jWaWWE jrLlAa"></span><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-jffHpj jWaWWE cThoNa">string</span><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-eJocfa jWaWWE bArHDh"> (<!-- -->DocKey<!-- -->) </span></div> <div><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr lhENGb"><p>A string id (UUID)</p>
</div></div></div></td></tr><tr class="last "><td class="sc-hBMUJo sc-fFSPTT iwcKgn cAqMTE" kind="field" title="tableId"><span class="sc-iemWCZ bcnRwz"></span><span class="property-name">tableId</span><div class="sc-oeezt sc-hhIiOg dLCGMn hIkHYw">required</div></td><td class="sc-bkbkJK ctPuOP"><div><div><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-iNiQyp jWaWWE jrLlAa"></span><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-jffHpj jWaWWE cThoNa">string</span></div> <div><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr lhENGb"><p>name of a table (normalized)</p>
</div></div></div></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div><h5 class="sc-iqAclL eONCmm">query<!-- --> Parameters</h5><table class="sc-hHEiqL VCQHZ"><tbody><tr class=""><td class="sc-hBMUJo sc-fFSPTT iwcKgn cAqMTE" kind="field" title="filter"><span class="sc-iemWCZ bcnRwz"></span><span class="property-name">filter</span></td><td class="sc-bkbkJK ctPuOP"><div><div><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-iNiQyp jWaWWE jrLlAa"></span><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-jffHpj jWaWWE cThoNa">string</span></div> <div><span class="sc-laZMeE jWaWWE"> <!-- -->Example:<!-- --> </span> <span class="sc-laZMeE sc-ckTSus jWaWWE fElSEN">filter={&quot;pet&quot;: [&quot;cat&quot;, &quot;dog&quot;]}</span></div><div><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr lhENGb"><p>This is a JSON object mapping column names to arrays of allowed values.  For example, to filter column <code>pet</code> for values <code>cat</code> and <code>dog</code>, the filter would be <code>{&quot;pet&quot;: [&quot;cat&quot;, &quot;dog&quot;]}</code>. JSON contains characters that are not safe to place in a URL, so it is important to url-encode them.  For this example, the url-encoding is <code>%7B%22pet%22%3A%20%5B%22cat%22%2C%20%22dog%22%5D%7D</code>. See <a href="https://rosettacode.org/wiki/URL_encoding">https://rosettacode.org/wiki/URL_encoding</a> for how to url-encode a string, or <a href="https://www.urlencoder.org/">https://www.urlencoder.org/</a> to try some examples. Multiple columns can be filtered. For example the filter for <code>pet</code> being either <code>cat</code> or <code>dog</code>, AND <code>size</code> being either <code>tiny</code> or <code>outrageously small</code>, would be <code>{&quot;pet&quot;: [&quot;cat&quot;, &quot;dog&quot;], &quot;size&quot;: [&quot;tiny&quot;, &quot;outrageously small&quot;]}</code>.</p>
</div></div></div></td></tr><tr class=""><td class="sc-hBMUJo sc-fFSPTT iwcKgn cAqMTE" kind="field" title="sort"><span class="sc-iemWCZ bcnRwz"></span><span class="property-name">sort</span></td><td class="sc-bkbkJK ctPuOP"><div><div><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-iNiQyp jWaWWE jrLlAa"></span><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-jffHpj jWaWWE cThoNa">string</span></div> <div><span class="sc-laZMeE jWaWWE"> <!-- -->Example:<!-- --> </span> <span class="sc-laZMeE sc-ckTSus jWaWWE fElSEN">sort=pet,-age</span></div><div><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr lhENGb"><p>Order in which to return results. If a single column name is given (e.g. <code>pet</code>), results are placed in ascending order of values in that column. To get results in an order that was previously prepared manually in Grist, use the special <code>manualSort</code> column name. Multiple columns can be specified, separated by commas (e.g. <code>pet,age</code>). For descending order, prefix a column name with a <code>-</code> character (e.g. <code>pet,-age</code>). To include additional sorting options append them after a colon (e.g. <code>pet,-age:naturalSort;emptyFirst,owner</code>). Available options are: <code>choiceOrder</code>, <code>naturalSort</code>, <code>emptyFirst</code>. Without the <code>sort</code> parameter, the order of results is unspecified.</p>
</div></div></div></td></tr><tr class="last "><td class="sc-hBMUJo sc-fFSPTT iwcKgn cAqMTE" kind="field" title="limit"><span class="sc-iemWCZ bcnRwz"></span><span class="property-name">limit</span></td><td class="sc-bkbkJK ctPuOP"><div><div><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-iNiQyp jWaWWE jrLlAa"></span><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-jffHpj jWaWWE cThoNa">number</span></div> <div><span class="sc-laZMeE jWaWWE"> <!-- -->Example:<!-- --> </span> <span class="sc-laZMeE sc-ckTSus jWaWWE fElSEN">limit=5</span></div><div><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr lhENGb"><p>Return at most this number of rows.  A value of 0 is equivalent to having no limit.</p>
</div></div></div></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div><h5 class="sc-iqAclL eONCmm">header<!-- --> Parameters</h5><table class="sc-hHEiqL VCQHZ"><tbody><tr class=""><td class="sc-hBMUJo sc-fFSPTT iwcKgn cAqMTE" kind="field" title="X-Sort"><span class="sc-iemWCZ bcnRwz"></span><span class="property-name">X-Sort</span></td><td class="sc-bkbkJK ctPuOP"><div><div><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-iNiQyp jWaWWE jrLlAa"></span><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-jffHpj jWaWWE cThoNa">string</span></div> <div><span class="sc-laZMeE jWaWWE"> <!-- -->Example:<!-- --> </span> <span class="sc-laZMeE sc-ckTSus jWaWWE fElSEN">pet,-age</span></div><div><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr lhENGb"><p>Same as <code>sort</code> query parameter.</p>
</div></div></div></td></tr><tr class="last "><td class="sc-hBMUJo sc-fFSPTT iwcKgn cAqMTE" kind="field" title="X-Limit"><span class="sc-iemWCZ bcnRwz"></span><span class="property-name">X-Limit</span></td><td class="sc-bkbkJK ctPuOP"><div><div><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-iNiQyp jWaWWE jrLlAa"></span><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-jffHpj jWaWWE cThoNa">number</span></div> <div><span class="sc-laZMeE jWaWWE"> <!-- -->Example:<!-- --> </span> <span class="sc-laZMeE sc-ckTSus jWaWWE fElSEN">5</span></div><div><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr lhENGb"><p>Same as <code>limit</code> query parameter.</p>
</div></div></div></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div><h3 class="sc-fIxmyt DvFer">Responses</h3><div><button class="sc-htmcrh lbYftx"><svg class="sc-dIsUp dqYXmg" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 24 24" x="0" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" y="0" aria-hidden="true"><polygon points="17.3 8.3 12 13.6 6.7 8.3 5.3 9.7 12 16.4 18.7 9.7 "></polygon></svg><strong class="sc-fWWYYk cMoEZ">200<!-- --> </strong><span class="sc-jcwpoC eDjFAZ"><p>Cells from the table</p>

</h3><div class="sc-cxNHIi gxohHo" data-rttabs="true"><ul class="react-tabs__tab-list" role="tablist"><li class="tab-success react-tabs__tab--selected" role="tab" id="react-tabs-62" aria-selected="true" aria-disabled="false" aria-controls="react-tabs-63" tabindex="0" data-rttab="true">200</li></ul><div class="react-tabs__tab-panel react-tabs__tab-panel--selected" role="tabpanel" id="react-tabs-63" aria-labelledby="react-tabs-62"><div><div class="sc-Arkif jojbRz"><span class="sc-cOifOu hlhNtL">Content type</span><div class="sc-bBjRSN kQSIAz">application/json</div></div><div class="sc-jgPyTC dSaTNC"><div class="sc-jNnpgg esZIbL"><div class="sc-giAqHp hMPeqJ"><button><div class="sc-carFqZ UksDl">Copy</div></button></div><div class="sc-iJCRrE jCdxGr sc-dPaNzc gyljjx"><div class="redoc-json"><code><span class="token keyword">null</span></code></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div id="tag/attachments" data-section-id="tag/attachments" class="sc-eCApnc lpoiLM"><div class="sc-iCoGMd fStpoi"><div class="sc-hKFxyN bwFyQs"><h1 class="sc-fujyAs bpZWeL"><a class="sc-crzoAE iUxAWq" href="#tag/attachments" aria-label="tag/attachments"></a>/attachments</h1></div></div><div class="sc-hKFxyN lksXXu"><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr QGruV redoc-markdown "><p>Documents may include attached files. Data records can refer to these using a column of type <code>Attachments</code>.</p>
</div></div></div><div id="tag/attachments/paths/~1docs~1{docId}~1attachments/get" data-section-id="tag/attachments/paths/~1docs~1{docId}~1attachments/get" class="sc-eCApnc khndJD"><div class="sc-iCoGMd fStpoi"><div class="sc-hKFxyN bwFyQs"><h2 class="sc-pNWdM eftmgB"><a class="sc-crzoAE iUxAWq" href="#tag/attachments/paths/~1docs~1{docId}~1attachments/get" aria-label="tag/attachments/paths/~1docs~1{docId}~1attachments/get"></a>List metadata of all attachments in a doc<!-- --> </h2><div class="sc-EZqKI fWsqvQ"><button class="sc-eEVmNe hyDbyC"><span type="get" class="sc-fmdNqN ihNycv http-verb get">get</span><span class="sc-jXcxbT fCEUju">/docs/{docId}/attachments</span><svg class="sc-dIsUp izTTdU" style="margin-right:-25px" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 24 24" x="0" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" y="0" aria-hidden="true"><polygon points="17.3 8.3 12 13.6 6.7 8.3 5.3 9.7 12 16.4 18.7 9.7 "></polygon></svg></button><div aria-hidden="true" class="sc-ljsmAU flIrdF"><div class="sc-jlZJtj fQkroN"><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr lhENGb"></div><div tabindex="0" role="button"><div class="sc-dTSzeu dfUAUz"><span>https://docs.getgrist.com/api</span>/docs/{docId}/attachments</div></div></div><div class="sc-jlZJtj fQkroN"><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr lhENGb"></div><div tabindex="0" role="button"><div class="sc-dTSzeu dfUAUz"><span>https://&lt;TEAM&gt;.getgrist.com/api</span>/docs/{docId}/attachments</div></div></div></div></div><div class="sc-fcmMJX cvfxAX"><div class="sc-jUfyBS bhDyou"><h5 class="sc-iqAclL sc-fuISkM eONCmm hZIgic">Authorizations:</h5><svg class="sc-dIsUp iPqByX" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 24 24" x="0" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" y="0" aria-hidden="true"><polygon points="17.3 8.3 12 13.6 6.7 8.3 5.3 9.7 12 16.4 18.7 9.7 "></polygon></svg></div><div class="sc-jQAxuV ccffaZ"><span class="sc-daBunf fcvuS"><span class="sc-dsXzNU dPrSxx"><i>API Key</i></span></span></div></div><div><h5 class="sc-iqAclL eONCmm">path<!-- --> Parameters</h5><table class="sc-hHEiqL VCQHZ"><tbody><tr class="last "><td class="sc-hBMUJo sc-fFSPTT iwcKgn cAqMTE" kind="field" title="docId"><span class="sc-iemWCZ bcnRwz"></span><span class="property-name">docId</span><div class="sc-oeezt sc-hhIiOg dLCGMn hIkHYw">required</div></td><td class="sc-bkbkJK ctPuOP"><div><div><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-iNiQyp jWaWWE jrLlAa"></span><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-jffHpj jWaWWE cThoNa">string</span><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-eJocfa jWaWWE bArHDh"> (<!-- -->DocKey<!-- -->) </span></div> <div><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr lhENGb"><p>A string id (UUID)</p>
</div></div></div></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div><h5 class="sc-iqAclL eONCmm">query<!-- --> Parameters</h5><table class="sc-hHEiqL VCQHZ"><tbody><tr class=""><td class="sc-hBMUJo sc-fFSPTT iwcKgn cAqMTE" kind="field" title="filter"><span class="sc-iemWCZ bcnRwz"></span><span class="property-name">filter</span></td><td class="sc-bkbkJK ctPuOP"><div><div><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-iNiQyp jWaWWE jrLlAa"></span><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-jffHpj jWaWWE cThoNa">string</span></div> <div><span class="sc-laZMeE jWaWWE"> <!-- -->Example:<!-- --> </span> <span class="sc-laZMeE sc-ckTSus jWaWWE fElSEN">filter={&quot;pet&quot;: [&quot;cat&quot;, &quot;dog&quot;]}</span></div><div><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr lhENGb"><p>This is a JSON object mapping column names to arrays of allowed values.  For example, to filter column <code>pet</code> for values <code>cat</code> and <code>dog</code>, the filter would be <code>{&quot;pet&quot;: [&quot;cat&quot;, &quot;dog&quot;]}</code>. JSON contains characters that are not safe to place in a URL, so it is important to url-encode them.  For this example, the url-encoding is <code>%7B%22pet%22%3A%20%5B%22cat%22%2C%20%22dog%22%5D%7D</code>. See <a href="https://rosettacode.org/wiki/URL_encoding">https://rosettacode.org/wiki/URL_encoding</a> for how to url-encode a string, or <a href="https://www.urlencoder.org/">https://www.urlencoder.org/</a> to try some examples. Multiple columns can be filtered. For example the filter for <code>pet</code> being either <code>cat</code> or <code>dog</code>, AND <code>size</code> being either <code>tiny</code> or <code>outrageously small</code>, would be <code>{&quot;pet&quot;: [&quot;cat&quot;, &quot;dog&quot;], &quot;size&quot;: [&quot;tiny&quot;, &quot;outrageously small&quot;]}</code>.</p>
</div></div></div></td></tr><tr class=""><td class="sc-hBMUJo sc-fFSPTT iwcKgn cAqMTE" kind="field" title="sort"><span class="sc-iemWCZ bcnRwz"></span><span class="property-name">sort</span></td><td class="sc-bkbkJK ctPuOP"><div><div><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-iNiQyp jWaWWE jrLlAa"></span><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-jffHpj jWaWWE cThoNa">string</span></div> <div><span class="sc-laZMeE jWaWWE"> <!-- -->Example:<!-- --> </span> <span class="sc-laZMeE sc-ckTSus jWaWWE fElSEN">sort=pet,-age</span></div><div><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr lhENGb"><p>Order in which to return results. If a single column name is given (e.g. <code>pet</code>), results are placed in ascending order of values in that column. To get results in an order that was previously prepared manually in Grist, use the special <code>manualSort</code> column name. Multiple columns can be specified, separated by commas (e.g. <code>pet,age</code>). For descending order, prefix a column name with a <code>-</code> character (e.g. <code>pet,-age</code>). To include additional sorting options append them after a colon (e.g. <code>pet,-age:naturalSort;emptyFirst,owner</code>). Available options are: <code>choiceOrder</code>, <code>naturalSort</code>, <code>emptyFirst</code>. Without the <code>sort</code> parameter, the order of results is unspecified.</p>
</div></div></div></td></tr><tr class="last "><td class="sc-hBMUJo sc-fFSPTT iwcKgn cAqMTE" kind="field" title="limit"><span class="sc-iemWCZ bcnRwz"></span><span class="property-name">limit</span></td><td class="sc-bkbkJK ctPuOP"><div><div><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-iNiQyp jWaWWE jrLlAa"></span><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-jffHpj jWaWWE cThoNa">number</span></div> <div><span class="sc-laZMeE jWaWWE"> <!-- -->Example:<!-- --> </span> <span class="sc-laZMeE sc-ckTSus jWaWWE fElSEN">limit=5</span></div><div><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr lhENGb"><p>Return at most this number of rows.  A value of 0 is equivalent to having no limit.</p>
</div></div></div></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div><h5 class="sc-iqAclL eONCmm">header<!-- --> Parameters</h5><table class="sc-hHEiqL VCQHZ"><tbody><tr class=""><td class="sc-hBMUJo sc-fFSPTT iwcKgn cAqMTE" kind="field" title="X-Sort"><span class="sc-iemWCZ bcnRwz"></span><span class="property-name">X-Sort</span></td><td class="sc-bkbkJK ctPuOP"><div><div><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-iNiQyp jWaWWE jrLlAa"></span><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-jffHpj jWaWWE cThoNa">string</span></div> <div><span class="sc-laZMeE jWaWWE"> <!-- -->Example:<!-- --> </span> <span class="sc-laZMeE sc-ckTSus jWaWWE fElSEN">pet,-age</span></div><div><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr lhENGb"><p>Same as <code>sort</code> query parameter.</p>

See https://rosettacode.org/wiki/URL_encoding for how to url-encode a string, or https://www.urlencoder.org/ to try some examples. Multiple columns can be filtered. For descending order, prefix a column name with a `-` character (e.g. `pet,-age`). To include additional sorting options append them after a colon (e.g. `pet,-age:naturalSort;emptyFirst,owner`).
